[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m16582[0m[39m:    [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m5[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m10[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m20[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m40[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m64[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m80[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m128[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m160[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m256[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m320[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m512[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m640[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m16583[0m[39m:  [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m;[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m16584[0m[39m:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m16585[0m[39m:  return vals[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39midx, [0m[1;35marray_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvals[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m16586[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mepan/dissectors/packet-netbios.[0m[1;92mc:1106[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1108[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1106[0m[39m:   [0m[39mcommand = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39m tvb, offset + NB_COMMAND[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1107[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* limit command so no table overflows *[0m[35m/[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1108[0m[39m:   [0m[39mcommand = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcommand, [0m[1;35marray_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdissect_netb[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mepan/dissectors/packet-netbios.[0m[1;92mc:577[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m585[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m577[0m[39m:static uint32_t[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m578:d[0m[1;35missect_netb_unknown[0m[1;39m([0m[39m tvbuff_t *tvb, packet_info *pinfo, int offset, proto_tree[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m*tree[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m579[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m580[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m[35m/[0m[39m* Handle any unknown commands, do nothing *[0m[35m/[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m581[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m582[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_expert[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtree, pinfo, &ei_netb_unknown_command_data, tvb, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset + NB_COMMAND + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m-1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m583[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m584[0m[39m:    [0m[39mreturn [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m585[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause Identification[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe global-buffer-overflow vulnerability is caused by an **off-by-one error** in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe bounds checking logic at line [0m[1;36m1108[0m[39m of `packet-netbios.c`. [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Key Facts:**[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The `dissect_netb` function pointer array has [0m[1;36m33[0m[39m elements [0m[1;39m([0m[39mindices [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m32[0m[1;39m)[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Line [0m[1;36m1108[0m[39m uses `command = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcommand, [0m[1;35marray_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdissect_netb[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which caps [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe command at [0m[1;36m33[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Line [0m[1;36m1144[0m[39m accesses `dissect_netb[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mcommand[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, which attempts to read index [0m[1;36m33[0m[39m when[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcommand >= [0m[1;36m33[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Valid C array indices are [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m to [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m to [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m for this array[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. The test case has command byte [0m[1;36m0xfa[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m250[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which gets capped to [0m[1;36m33[0m[39m, causing the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout-of-bounds read[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Memory Layout:**[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `dissect_netb` is a [0m[1;36m264[0m[39m-byte global array [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m33[0m[39m function pointers × [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes each on[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m-bit[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Index [0m[1;36m33[0m[39m is [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes beyond the array boundary[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- AddressSanitizer correctly detects the [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte read at the invalid address[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Code Context[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe `dissect_netb` array contains function pointers for handling NetBIOS commands [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0x00[0m[39m through [0m[1;36m0x1f[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mindices [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, with an additional `dissect_netb_unknown` handler[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mat index [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m to gracefully handle any undefined commands within the array bounds.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe intent of line [0m[1;36m1108[0m[39m's comment [0m[32m"/* limit command so no table overflows */"[0m[39m was [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto prevent buffer overflow, but the implementation is incorrect due to the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moff-by-one error.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Existing Codebase Pattern[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe Wireshark codebase already has correct implementations of this pattern in [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`packet-lte-rrc.c`:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreturn vals[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39midx, [0m[1;35marray_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvals[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis pattern ensures the index never exceeds the last valid array index, and [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomments indicate the intent to [0m[32m"return last element of array"[0m[39m for out-of-range [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindices.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix Location[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File:** `epan/dissectors/packet-netbios.c`  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Line:** [0m[1;36m1108[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change from:**[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcommand = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcommand, [0m[1;35marray_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdissect_netb[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change to:**[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcommand = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcommand, [0m[1;35marray_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdissect_netb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Fix Is Optimal[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal Change:** Single-character modification [0m[1;39m([0m[32m"-1"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with zero risk of [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbreaking existing functionality[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Preserves Design Intent:** [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The array already has `dissect_netb_unknown` at index [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m as a fallback[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Invalid commands [0m[1;39m([0m[39m>= [0m[1;36m32[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will now correctly map to this handler[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The comment [0m[32m"/* limit command so no table overflows */"[0m[39m remains accurate[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Follows Established Pattern:** Matches the proven pattern used in [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`packet-lte-rrc.c` and elsewhere in the codebase[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Maintains Existing Logic:**[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All valid commands [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0x00[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m0x1f[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continue to map to their specific handlers[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Unknown commands within bounds [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0x04[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m0x06[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0x0B[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m0x0C[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0x10[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m0x12[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0x1D[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m0x1E[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malready map to `dissect_netb_unknown`[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Out-of-bounds commands now safely map to index [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dissect_netb_unknown`[0m[1;39m)[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Complete Fix:** Addresses the root cause directly without requiring changes [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39melsewhere[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Prevents the Vulnerability[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Before Fix:**[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Command value [0m[1;36m0xfa[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m250[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m → [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m250[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m33[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m → [0m[1;36m33[0m[39m → `dissect_netb[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m33[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` → **buffer [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow**[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**After Fix:**[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Command value [0m[1;36m0xfa[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m250[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m → [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m250[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m32[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m → [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m → `dissect_netb[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m32[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39m= [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_netb_unknown`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m → **safe access**[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe `dissect_netb_unknown` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m577[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m585[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m handles unknown commands [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgracefully by adding an expert info item to the protocol tree and returning [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich is the intended behavior for undefined commands.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### No Side Effects[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **No Functional Changes:** All existing command handlers remain unchanged[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **No Test Breakage:** The fix only affects out-of-bounds command values, which [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwere already buggy[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No Performance Impact:** Single integer comparison, no additional overhead[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No API Changes:** Function signatures and calling conventions remain identical[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Fuzzing Compatibility:** The fix supports the same fuzzing logic and entry [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpoints[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Validation[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix can be validated by:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
